          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;

          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }
        .container-no-issue {
          padding: 0.5em 16px;
          font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
        }
        .metadata-container {
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          background: var(--monorail-metadata-toggled-bg);
          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);

          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          box-sizing: border-box;

        }
        .issue-header-container {
          z-index: 10;

          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;
        }

          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;
          flex-grow: 1;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          min-height: 100%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
        }
        mr-issue-metadata {
          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }
        mr-launch-overview {
          border-left: var(--chops-normal-border);

          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





When making a search in |string_id_map_|[1], there is no check whether the query result is end(). The out of bounds will occur when using |string_id_map_.end()|.



<span class="line"><!---->When making a search in |string_id_map_|[1], there is no check whether the query result is end(). The out of bounds will occur when using |string_id_map_.end()|.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1]. 



<span class="line"><!---->[1]. <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc;l=197;drc=354945de1fb564ef04c07cf8bfedf434d2d81747



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc;l=197;drc=354945de1fb564ef04c07cf8bfedf434d2d81747"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc;l=197;drc=354945de1fb564ef04c07cf8bfedf434d2d81747<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





Fix suggestion:



<span class="line"><!---->Fix suggestion:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





diff --git a/ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc b/ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc



<span class="line"><!---->diff --git a/ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc b/ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc<!----></span>



<br>





index 52aafdd8b820b..e71f8c18259ae 100644



<span class="line"><!---->index 52aafdd8b820b..e71f8c18259ae 100644<!----></span>



<br>





--- a/ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc



<span class="line"><!---->--- a/ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc<!----></span>



<br>





+++ b/ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc



<span class="line"><!---->+++ b/ash/webui/scanning/scanning_handler.cc<!----></span>



<br>





@@ -193,6 +193,9 @@ void ScanningHandler::HandleGetPluralString(const base::ListValue* args) {



<span class="line"><!---->@@ -193,6 +193,9 @@ void ScanningHandler::HandleGetPluralString(const base::ListValue* args) {<!----></span>



<br>





   const std::string name = args->GetListDeprecated()[1].GetString();



<span class="line"><!---->   const std::string name = args-&gt;GetListDeprecated()[1].GetString();<!----></span>



<br>





   const int count = args->GetListDeprecated()[2].GetInt();



<span class="line"><!---->   const int count = args-&gt;GetListDeprecated()[2].GetInt();<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





+  if (string_id_map_.find(name) == string_id_map_.end())



<span class="line"><!---->+  if (string_id_map_.find(name) == string_id_map_.end())<!----></span>



<br>





+    return;



<span class="line"><!---->+    return;<!----></span>



<br>





+  



<span class="line"><!---->+  <!----></span>



<br>





   const std::u16string localized_string = l10n_util::GetPluralStringFUTF16(



<span class="line"><!---->   const std::u16string localized_string = l10n_util::GetPluralStringFUTF16(<!----></span>



<br>





       string_id_map_.find(name)->second, count);



<span class="line"><!---->       string_id_map_.find(name)-&gt;second, count);<!----></span>



<br>





   ResolveJavascriptCallback(base::Value(callback),



<span class="line"><!---->   ResolveJavascriptCallback(base::Value(callback),<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: stable<!----></span>

<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>

<span class="line"><!---->browsing `chrome://scanning` and open devtools<!----></span>

, 



<span class="line"><!---->, <!----></span>





this would benefit from a ReceivedBadMessage() method for non-mojo WebUI handlers. ReceivedBadMessage() would be more appropriate here rather than silently ignoring with early return.



<span class="line"><!---->this would benefit from a ReceivedBadMessage() method for non-mojo WebUI handlers. ReceivedBadMessage() would be more appropriate here rather than silently ignoring with early return.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

Hello leecraso and thank you for this report. As this issue requires user interaction and appears to result in a read, the VRP Panel has decided to award you $3,000 for this report. If you can demonstrate more impactful memory corruption resulting from this issue, we would be happy to reassess. Thanks again for your efforts and reporting this issue to us!



<span class="line"><!---->Hello leecraso and thank you for this report. If you can demonstrate more impactful memory corruption resulting from this issue, we would be happy to reassess. Thanks again for your efforts and reporting this issue to us!<!----></span>
